Effective October 30, travellers will need to be fully vaccinated in order to board. Specifically, the vaccination requirement will apply to all travellers 12 years of age and older who are:

Air passengers flying on domestic, transborder or international flights departing from airports in Canada
Rail passengers on VIA Rail and Rocky Mountaineer trains
Marine passengers on non-essential passenger vessels, such as cruise ships, on voyages of 24 hours or more

This is apparantly an email from a leaker from the liberal party of Canada. The isolation centers we already know are being built as shown on the gov website RFP program.

Fw: LPC Strategic Committee Leak
Inbox
LPC leaker <LPC_leaker@protonmail.com>

1:47 PM (7 hours ago)
‚Äê‚Äê‚Äê‚Äê‚Äê Original Message ‚Äê‚Äê‚Äê‚Äê‚Äê‚Äê‚Äê
On Saturday, October 10, 2020 1:38 PM, REMOVED <REMOVED> wrote:

> Dear REMOVED,
I want to provide you some very important information. I'm a committee member within the Liberal Party of Canada. I sit within several committee groups but the information I am providing is originating from the Strategic Planning committee (which is steered by the PMO).
>
> I need to start off by saying that I'm not happy doing this but I have to. As a Canadian and more importantly as a parent who wants a better future not only for my children but for other children as well. The other reason I am doing this is because roughly 30% of the committee members are not pleased with the direction this will take Canada, but our opinions have been ignored and they plan on moving forward toward their goals. They have also made it very clear that nothing will stop the planned outcomes.
>
> The road map and aim was set out by the PMO and is as follows:
>
> - Phase in secondary lock down restrictions on a rolling basis, starting with major metropolitan areas first and expanding outward. Expected by November 2020.
> - Rush the acquisition of (or construction of) isolation facilities across every province and territory. Expected by December 2020.
> - Daily new cases of COVID-19 will surge beyond capacity of testing, including increases in COVID related deaths following the same growth curves. Expected by end of November 2020.
> - Complete and total secondary lock down (much stricter than the first and second rolling phase restrictions). Expected by end of December 2020 - early January 2021
> - Reform and expansion of the unemployment program to be transitioned into the universal basic income program. Expected by Q1 2021.
> - Projected COVID-19 mutation and/or co-infection with secondary virus (referred to as COVID-21) leading to a third wave with much higher mortality rate and higher rate of infection. Expected by February 2021.
> - Daily new cases of COVID-21 hospitalizations and COVID-19 and COVID-21 related deaths will exceed medical care facilities capacity. Expected Q1 - Q2 2021.
> - Enhanced lock down restrictions (referred to as Third Lock Down) will be implemented. Full travel restrictions will be imposed (including inter-province and inter-city). Expected Q2 2021.
> - Transitioning of individuals into the universal basic income program. Expected mid Q2 2021.
> - Projected supply chain break downs, inventory shortages, large economic instability. Expected late Q2 2021.
> - Deployment of military personnel into major metropolitan areas as well as all major roadways to establish travel checkpoints. Restrict travel and movement. Provide logistical support to the area. Expected by Q3 2021.
>
>
>
> Along with that provided road map the Strategic Planning committee was asked to design an effective way of transitioning Canadians to meet a unprecedented economic endeavor. One that would change the face of Canada and forever alter the lives of Canadians. What we were told was that in order to offset what was essentially an economic collapse on a international scale, that the federal government was going to offer Canadians a total debt relief. This is how it works: the federal government will offer to eliminate all personal debts (mortgages, loans, credit cards, etc) which all funding will be provided
> to Canada by the IMF under what will become known as the World Debt Reset program. In exchange for acceptance of this total debt forgiveness the individual would forfeit ownership of any and all property and assets forever.
23:52
The individual would also have to agree to partake in the COVID-19 and COVID-21 vaccination schedule, which would provide the individual with unrestricted travel and unrestricted living even under a full lock down (through the use of photo identification referred to as Canada's HealthPass) .
>
> Committee members asked who would become the owner of the forfeited property and assets in that scenario and what would happen to lenders or financial institutions, we were simply told "the World Debt Reset program will handle all of the details". Several committee members also questioned what would happen to individuals if they refused to participate in the World Debt Reset program, or the HealthPass, or the vaccination schedule, and the answer we got was very troubling. Essentially we were told it was our duty to make sure we came up with a plan to ensure that would never happen. We were told it was in the individuals best interest to participate. When several committee members pushed relentlessly to get an answer we were told that those who refused would first live under the lock down restrictions indefinitely. And that over a short period of time as more Canadians transitioned into the debt forgiveness program, the ones who refused to participate would be deemed a public safety risk and would be relocated into isolation facilities. Once in those facilities they would be given two options, participate in the debt forgiveness program and be released, or stay indefinitely in the isolation facility under the classification of a serious public health risk and have all their assets seized.
>
> So as you can imagine after hearing all of this it turned into quite the heated discussion and escalated beyond anything I've ever witnessed before. In the end it was implied by the PMO that the whole agenda will move forward no matter who agrees with it or not. That it wont just be Canada but in fact all nations will have similar roadmaps and agendas. That we need to take advantage of the situations before us to promote change on a grander scale for the betterment of everyone. The members who were opposed and ones who brought up key issues that would arise from such a thing were completely ignored. Our opinions and concerns were ignored. We were simply told to just do it.
>
>
> All I know is that I don't like it and I think its going to place Canadians into a dark future.
>
7 October 2021

This is our protest against the regulations, restrictions of basic laws related to the C virus *. We do this on October 12, 2021, we turn off all devices between 4:00 and 4:21 pm for 21 minutes and cut all electricity. –ù–æ –∑–∞–∫–æ–Ω–Ω–æ –ª–∏ —ç—Ç–æ? –ú–æ–∂–µ–º –ª–∏ –º—ã –ø–æ–º–µ—à–∞—Ç—å –∏–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—Ü—É, –∂–∏–≤—É—â–µ–º—É –≤ –ö–∞–Ω–∞–¥–µ, –≤–µ—Ä–Ω—É—Ç—å—Å—è –¥–æ–º–æ–π? –î–∞, –ø–æ —Å–ª–æ–≤–∞–º –ú–µ –§—Ä–∞–Ω—Å—É–∞ –ö—Ä–µ–ø–æ, —ç–∫—Å–ø–µ—Ä—Ç–∞ –≤ –æ–±–ª–∞—Å—Ç–∏ –º–µ–∂–¥—É–Ω–∞—Ä–æ–¥–Ω–æ–≥–æ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∞, –Ω–æ —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –ø—Ä–∏ –æ–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö —É—Å–ª–æ–≤–∏—è—Ö.

–ù–∞ —Å–∫–æ–ª –∫–æ –º–Ω–µ –∏–∑–≤–µ—Å—Ç–Ω–æ –ê–≤—Å—Ç—Ä–∞–ª–∏—è —É–∂–µ –¥–∞–≤–Ω–æ –Ω–∏–∫–æ–≥–æ –Ω–µ –≤–ø—É—Å–∫–∞–µ—Ç –∏ –Ω–µ –≤—ã–ø—É—Å–∫–∞–µ—Ç –±–µ–∑ —Å–ø–µ—Ü —Ä–∞–∑—Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏—è.
–î–∞–∂–µ –≥—Ä–∞–∂–¥–∞–Ω–µ –Ω–µ –º–æ–≥—É—Ç –ø–æ–ø–∞—Å—Ç—å –¥–æ–º–æ–π.

Vaccine Choice Canada 12.10.2021 10:36:44
When I was in training at the Royal Alex hospital, we bathed babies within hours after their birth (as long as their temperature was in the normal range). Now, standard of practice is to wait 24 hours after birth.That's a whole day! All because someone challenged this common practice and showed that there was a better way! They showed that babies do better if given longer to adjust to the outside world before being bathed. Because there was a better way, practice changed.
Imagine a health care system where new information is stifled if it doesn't conform to previously held beliefs/information.
Pretty stagnant at best.
Deadly at worst.

Now imagine that all the professionals who have the courage to ask the unpopular questions, and who are curious enough to look at the other side of the coin, are all gone. Only those who agree with every AHS mandate are allowed to remain.
Now you have totalitarian healthcare.
Deadly at best.
Genocidal at worst.

Nursing has always been a profession that fights for informed, voluntary consent.

We are all taught that patients have the right to refuse any medication or treatment. I have often been the one explaining to an anemic patient receiving blood for the first time, some of the risks and benefits of red blood cell transfusion. Countless times, I have returned prescribed medications to the med cart, because a patient refused to take them once they found out the purpose of the medication.

We called it Patient Autonomy.

Imagine if I forced all my patients to take every medication prescribed for them, even if they could cause harm, even if they suffered terrible side effects, and threatened to have the patients terminated from their jobs without pay if they didn't take said medications. This would be blatant coercion, a gross violation of my Code of Ethics, and justifiably, reason for professional punishment.

Yet, AHS is doing this very thing to every one of its employees and medical staff.

We are all being forced, under coercion and duress of losing our jobs, to take a medical treatment, to which we do NOT consent.

That violates Patient Autonomy, Informed Consent, and Right to Refuse.

I cannot ethically practice nursing for a company/government that has such disdain for patient autonomy.

I cannot ethically work for a company/government which will refuse pacemaker surgery to a patient simply because of their vaccination status.

I cannot ethically work for a company/government that tolerates obstetricians refusing care to pregnant mothers and their babies who choose to wait until after birth/breastfeeding to receive a vaccine that is NOT Category A in pregnancy.

I cannot ethically work for an employer which forces its employees to choose between receiving life-saving medication for their lethal illness as part of a clinical trial, vs. their job. (Taking the COVID-19 vaccine would require injecting a new substance into the body, thereby disqualifying the employee from their clinical trial). And yes, this is a real example of what an AHS employee is facing.

I cannot ethically work for a company that tells the public they are facing an unprecedented crisis necessitating lock down measures, while simultaneously threatening to place thousands of health care workers and doctors on unpaid Leave Of Absence. We have all safely worked, unvaccinated, for the duration of this pandemic, but now we will all be prohibited from providing care to our province, simply because of our vaccination status. What blatant disregard for our work, dedication, skill, and education. I am genuinely appalled at AHS' incredibly hypocritical treatment of its employees and physicians.

Therefore, I cannot and will not work for AHS so long as they mandate the COVID 19 vaccine to all their staff with such complete and utter disregard for personal choice, medical freedom, and informed consent.

Please consider this my official notice of resignation from my casual position as Registered Nurse at the QEII Hospital ER in Grande Prairie AB.

Sincerely,

Julianne Johnson BScN

Tonight, one MPP's private member's bill - Bill 12, An Act to Enact the Mandatory COVID-19 Vaccinations in the Education and Healthcare Sectors Act, 2021, is coming up for a vote at second reading at the Ontario legislature!

If Bill 12 were to pass tonight, it would be one vote away from becoming law.

Once enacted, Bill 12 would result in job loss for any employee of any organization in education or healthcare that does not wish to disclose their vaccine status!

Tonight, Bill 12 will be debated and voted on by Ontario MPPs.

Belinda will be at Queen's Park late tonight speaking and voting against Bill 12.

But the fate of Bill 12 lies with the majority PC MPPs who have each shown us next to no courage over the last three years.

Today, we need to push PC MPPs to find whatever little courage, if any, they have left, in order to vote against Bill 12.

Please take a couple of minutes this morning and call or email your MPP and ask them to vote against Bill 12, tonight!

Belinda will lead the charge at Queen's Park to stop Bill 12.

üí•üí•üí•üí• SHARE!! üí•üí•üí•üí•

RING RING RING‚òéÔ∏è HAVE YOU HAD YOUR VAXX TODAY???

SOME EXCELLENT ADVICE & QUESTIONS!
Shared from Bill Millar

I have heard of a number of unvaccinated people who have received calls prompting them to 'get the jab'. I think we should be prepared for the call. My thoughts.....

Ask questions, WRITE EVERYTHING DOWN.

What is your name? Please spell it for me.

How is it that you have access to my access to my health records?

Who gave you access to my health records? How do you spell their name?

Who authorized you to contact me? How do you spell their name?

Is there any aborted fetal cells used in the production of this vaccine? (There is, but write down their response.)

Please provide me with a list of the ingredients of this vaccine. (Make sure you write this down.)

Please provide me with a list of possible side effects.

What studies have been done determining risk verses benefits of the vaccine?

What recourse do I have if I happen to suffer from an adverse reaction?

How does natural immunity compare to immunity from the vaccine?

The list of questions could go on, but not sure it would get that far. If we all were to do this, would end these calls promptly.

A new airline is starting up with all the pilots and flight attendants who are walking out on mandates.

They are getting huge investors and starting a whole new travel model based on total sovereignty and medical freedom.

Why are they doing it?

"Our mission is to BE THE solution provider in the travel and transportation industry, as we believe in honoring everyone's right to travel freely, unencumbered, and without discrimination.

Our goal is to bring joy and wonder back into travel and the hospitality industry.

We are building an ecosystem of like-minded members, partners, and businesses to ensure and safeguard our rights as sovereign beings which includes the right to move about the world as a Freedom Traveler.

Join us as we celebrate and highlight these new partnerships with businesses, communities, cities, states and countries who align with our goals to preserve our inalienable rights."

Join Freedom Travel

Coronavirus masks are killing people, dentists warn

There is a new pandemic sweeping the country and its cause is persistent mask wearing.

‚ÄúMask mouth,‚Äù a play on meth mouth, is spreading like wildfire and dentists are warning that it could have serious consequences, including death.

‚ÄúGum disease, or periodontal disease, will eventually lead to strokes and an increased risk of heart attacks,‚Äù warns Marc Sclafani, a dentist and co-founder of One Manhattan Dental.

Wearing a mask on a regular basis is causing many to experience severe mouth inflammation, the complications of which can be extremely severe.

‚ÄúWe‚Äôre seeing inflammation in people‚Äôs gums that have been healthy forever, and cavities in people who have never had them before,‚Äù adds Rob Ramondi, another dentist and One Manhattan Dental co-founder.

According to Ramondi, roughly half of his patients are suffering from health problems due to wearing a mask.

‚ÄúAbout 50 percent of our patients are being impacted by this, so we decided to name it ‚Äòmask mouth‚Äô ‚Äì after ‚Äòmeth mouth.'‚Äù

Wearing a face covering breeds bacteria in front of the mouth and nose, where pathogens flourish in a warm, moist environment. These pathogens then enter the mouth and body, creating disease.

Another problem is mouth dryness, as people who wear a mask tend to breathe through the mouth while it is on rather than through the nose.

‚ÄúPeople tend to breathe through their mouth instead of through their nose while wearing a mask,‚Äù Sclafani says.

‚ÄúThe mouth breathing is causing the dry mouth, which leads to a decrease in saliva ‚Äì and saliva is what fights the bacteria and cleanses your teeth.‚Äù

Humans aren‚Äôt supposed to wear masks

It is almost as if the human body was not designed to wear a mask. When someone does is when the problems begin.

It is simply not healthy, no matter what the government or large corporations say, to block one‚Äôs breathing passages with fabric or plastic, especially the kind that is made in China.

There is no scientific evidence to show that wearing a mask does anything beneficial. In fact, the latest research shows that wearing a mask does pretty much nothing.

Why, then, are many politicians, big corporations, and media talking-heads still pushing them? The answer is anyone‚Äôs guess.

Those who are forced to wear a mask at work can try to drink more water and cut down on caffeine to help protect themselves against mask mouth. Sclafani also recommends that mask wearers use a humidifier, refrain from smoking, use an alcohol-free mouthwash, and scrape their tongue to further decrease their risk of complications.

Until a critical mass of Americans says enough is enough and take off the mask, the problem will only continue. In the coming months and years, expect to see a pandemic of oral health problems, heart problems, and early death caused by mask mouth.

The establishment will blame it all on the Wuhan coronavirus (Covid-19), of course, but do not be fooled: masks are the culprit.

‚ÄúPatients are coming into us like, ‚ÄòWow, my breath smells, I need a cleaning.‚Äô But when you smell the bad breath, you either already have periodontal disease or you have a lot of bacteria that‚Äôs sitting on your tongue because of dry mouth,‚Äù Sclafani further explains.

Sclafani encourages his patients to breathe through the nose whenever possible, but this is difficult for many mask wearers due to lack of oxygen and excess recycled carbon dioxide waste inside the mask.

‚ÄúMasks are unhealthy,‚Äù one Fox News commenter wrote. ‚ÄúIt increases the amount of carbon dioxide you breathe in. It is also a germ catcher that absorbs all the germs your hands touch.‚Äù

Dr. Simon 20.11.2021 13:20:12
COVID-19: stigmatising the unvaccinated is not justified

"There is increasing evidence that vaccinated individuals continue to have a relevant role in transmission. In Massachusetts, USA, a total of 469 new COVID-19 cases were detected during various events in July, 2021, and 346 (74%) of these cases were in people who were fully or partly vaccinated, 274 (79%) of whom were symptomatic.

[...]

It is therefore wrong and dangerous to speak of a pandemic of the unvaccinated. Historically, both the USA and Germany have engendered negative experiences by stigmatising parts of the population for their skin colour or religion. I call on high-level officials and scientists to stop the inappropriate stigmatisation of unvaccinated people, who include our patients, colleagues, and other fellow citizens, and to put extra effort into bringing society together."

Link to the Article: https://www.thelancet.com/journals/lancet/article/PIIS0140-6736(21)02243-1/fulltext

My email to board about non consent for my child to be touched or spoken to about vaccines.
Send to classroom teacher, principal, superintendents:

Good Morning Everyone,

It is without prejudice I am sending this notice of non-consent to the recipients of this email. I have nothing but respect for the work you all do to support the academic, social and emotional growth of my daughter. My husband and myself cherish the sweet anecdotes and insightful observations our daughter regales us with about her school days spent in your care - we truly hope this inclusive environment remains this way. However, as a parent, it is my duty to proactively protect the interests of my children with defensive measures as outlined in my attached communication.

By no means do I think the NCDSB staff would usher my child to a pop-up vaccine clinic in lieu of my parental consent (expressed or otherwise implied); however, I also did not expect that Toronto would be coercing 12 year olds with ice cream to get inoculated on the street corner, no health card or parent needed. The simple fact that there is a mobile vaccine distributing bus in our area soliciting to the public and our high school students during school hours is incredibly unnerving to me. Naturally, I revert to being pragmatic and defensive when past Public Health practises have been sneaky and divisive.

Please pay close attention to the stipulations highlighted in yellow on the document presented:
‚Äú In no way, shape, or form is my child to be talked to about the COVID-19 vaccine, be at all talked to about the possibility of being vaccinated, or the pros of being vaccinated for COVID-19. ‚Äú

Please leave the topic of vaccinations out of your classrooms and assemblies. If such an event were to take place at the school my daughter attends I expect to be informed with sufficient notice so as to make alternative arrangements for my daughter not to attend.

Lastly, I require written acknowledgment of this agreement. Tommi will not be attending school until her father, Ryan, and myself feel our concerns have been acknowledged and there is mutually agreed upon compliance to these documents. It is paramount that as parents we feel we can safely entrust the care of our children to those who hold positions of fiduciary trust over our children.
In addition to this electronic communication, you will receive these documents by paper mail as well. I hope this underscores the severity and seriousness with which we take the contents of these documents.

Thank you for your time and consideration, everyone. We are looking forward to resolving this communication swiftly.

God Bless,
Aly and Ryan Ludzik

Peel region residents - you can simply fill out the request for delegation form here https://www.peelregion.ca/council/guide-for-delegations.asp and send it to them at council@peelregion.ca

A list of restaurants in Ontario that won't ask for a vaccine passport. Hopefully more will be added but it's a good start.
Nov. 7th 2021

(Please don't share the list on Facebook)

I found out unfortunately 1. Deli & Diner, 52. Amici, 70. The Bent Elbow, 71. Pebble's Family Buffet & 78. Moorefield Diner want you to wear a mask to the table. There might be more but I don't know. This is about passports. We need to use common sense. We can't say "oh, this place doesn't require", then someone goes in and causes a scene.

Unfortunately Sizzlin' - Owen Sound & Two Forks - Port Stanley not anymore.
